The Soviet Union's Stakhanovite Movement: Stalin's Speech Clarifies its Significance and Purpose, Raising Labor Productivity to Complete the Industrial Revolution

(Moscow) Stalin delivered the following speech at the All-Union Stakhanovite Movement Congress:

The Stakhanovite movement is not an ordinary movement of male and female workers, but one of the most glorious pages in the history of Soviet socialist construction. What is the significance of this movement? First, it is a new upsurge of socialist competition, a new and higher stage of socialist competition. Why is it new? Why is it higher? Because it is easily distinguished from the past stages of socialist competition. In the past three years, socialist competition did not necessarily maintain a necessary connection with new technologies. Strictly speaking, we did not have new technologies at that time, but in the current stage of socialist competition, the Stakhanovite movement has a necessary connection with new technologies. This movement cannot be imagined without new and higher technologies. Before you are figures such as Stakhanov, Busygin, Smetanin, Krivonoss, Boronin, and Vinogradov. They are all new people, new workers. They can now fully control their technology and advance it. We did not have such people three years ago. They are new and special people.

The purpose of the Stakhanovite movement is to exceed the current technical standards, exceed the current work capacity, and exceed the current production plans and balances. Therefore, they want to overcome the records that have already passed for our era and our new people. This movement breaks the old concepts of technology, breaks the old records of technology, old work capacity, and old production plans. It requires the establishment of new and high records, work capacity, and production plans.

It requires the completion of our industrial revolution. From this point of view, the Stakhanovite movement is deeply revolutionary in nature. Some people here have said that the Stakhanovite movement is a manifestation of new and higher technical standards, and a standard for socialist high labor productivity (which is absolutely impossible in capitalist society). This is absolutely correct.

How can capitalism destroy and overcome feudalism? Because it can produce higher labor productivity records and can make society obtain more products than feudal society. Capitalism overcomes feudalism because it makes society richer. How can and must socialism defeat the capitalist economic system? There is no other reason than that it can produce examples of higher labor productivity than the capitalist economic system, because it can provide society with more products compared to the capitalist economic system, and can make society richer. Some people believe that we can consolidate socialism on the basis of a poor life and average assets. This kind of opinion is absolutely incorrect. This is a petty-bourgeois socialist idea. In reality, if socialism wants to win, it must be based on higher labor productivity than capitalism, it must be based on abundant products and various commodities, and it must be based on the rich and cultural life of all members of society. However, if we want to achieve this goal, if we want to make our socialist society the most prosperous, then we must have higher labor productivity than the major capitalist countries. Otherwise, we will be in vain if we want abundant products and commodities.

The significance of the Stakhanovite movement lies in breaking the previous inadequate technical records, exceeding the labor productivity of the major capitalist countries, thereby creating the possibility of consolidating Soviet socialism even more, and the possibility of transforming our country into the most prosperous country. "Although, the significance of the Stakhanovite movement is not limited to this, it also prepares the premise for the transition of socialism to communism. The principle of socialism is to each according to his ability, to each according to his work (not to each according to his needs). It means that the cultural and technical level of the working class is not very high at that time, the contradiction between mental and physical labor still exists, and labor productivity has not yet produced abundant commodities, so at that time the society cannot distribute products according to each person's needs, but only determines their remuneration according to their amount of work.

"Communism is a higher stage in development. The principle of communism is to each according to his ability, to each according to his needs. The distribution of products is not based on the amount of work, but according to the needs of each member with a very high cultural level. It means that at that time the cultural and technical level of the working class has been extremely superior, enough to eliminate the contradiction between mental and physical labor, and labor productivity has been extremely improved, enough to guarantee abundant products, so at that time the distribution of products can be based on their needs.

Some say that the opposition between mental and physical labor can reduce the cultural and technical level of engineers, technicians, and mental laborers, and make the culture and technology of mental and physical labor at the same level, that is, to eliminate this opposition in this way. This is absolutely wrong. Only petty-bourgeois talkers can delusionally realize communism in this way. In fact, the elimination of the opposition between mental and physical labor can only be achieved by raising the cultural and technical level of the working class to be equal to that of engineering and technical experts. "If it is said that this kind of improvement is absolutely impossible, it is a ridiculous idea. Under the Soviet system, the country's productivity has been liberated from the shackles of capitalism, labor has been liberated from oppression and exploitation, the working class has already obtained political power, and the children of laborers have been given various opportunities to obtain full technical education. This kind of improvement is absolutely possible. Only by raising the culture and technology of the laboring class can the source of the contradiction between mental and physical labor be eliminated, and labor productivity can be improved to obtain the abundant commodities necessary for the transition from socialism to communism. There is no doubt about this.

"The Stakhanovite movement is enough to be a link in this kind of transformation, because it has opened up the beginning for raising the cultural and technical level of our country's laboring class, although it is still weak, it is still an end. The Stakhanovite movement is that the people can fully control the technology of their work and obtain the maximum limit of harvest from the technology. At present, there are only a few Stakhanovite movers, but who can doubt that they will soon increase tenfold? Stakhanovite movers are inventors in our industry. The Thai-Hahanovite movement represents the future of our industry. It contains the seeds of raising the cultural and technical level of the laboring class in the future. It has opened a road for us. Only by moving forward can we raise labor productivity to the highest level, so as to transform from socialism to communism and eliminate the opposition between mental and physical labor. Is this not obvious?

"We are now at the cradle of the Stakhanovite movement, at its beginning, and we must pay attention to some of the characteristics of the Stakhanovite movement; first, this movement seems to be spontaneous, almost entirely from the bottom up, and does not come from the coercion of the management offices of our various enterprises.

"Secondly, this movement, once started, immediately moves forward; regardless of the intentions of the management offices of our various enterprises, and even fighting against them. Precisely because it is spontaneous, precisely because it is from the bottom up, it is the most important and immeasurable movement of the present era. "Another characteristic of the Stakhanovite movement is that it is all over the country; and it does not develop gradually, but moves forward with the unparalleled speed of thunder and lightning. The Stakhanovite movement has become an absolutely mature event. How will this point be explained? What makes it develop so quickly?

What is the source of the Stakhanovite movement? There are at least four reasons:

"First, the Stakhanovite movement first came from the thorough improvement of the material living conditions of laborers. Comrades' lives have been improved. Life is happier than before; life is happy, and work must also improve. Then the output increases? Then there are heroes of working men and women. This is the most important source of the Stakhanovite movement. If we also have panic, also have the plague of unemployment in the working class, if our lives are bad, without happiness, without hope, then we will not have a Stakhanovite movement (applause). Our proletarian revolution is the only revolution in the world that can give people an opportunity to not only show its political results, but also show its material living results. "Only our revolution, not only destroys the shackles of capitalism and gives people freedom, but also gives people the material conditions for a glorious life. This contains the power and invincibility of our revolution. This is why our life is so joyful, and why the Stakhanovite movement occurred.

"Second, the Stakhanovite movement is due to the elimination of the exploitation system in our country. The people of our country do not work for exploiters, do not work for wealthy non-laborers, but work for themselves, for their own class, for their excellent people, that is, for the Soviet society where the laboring class holds political power. This is why our work can have social significance, and it is a noble and glorious cause. Under capitalism, labor is of a private nature, so human labor under capitalism is not valued. In this case, it is clear that there cannot be a Stakhanovite movement. "There is another event about the Soviet system. Laborers here are respected, laborers here are not despised, and do not feel lonely. On the contrary, laborers and we all feel that we are free people of our own country, a social worker, and if their work is excellent, they can do their best to society, they are a labor hero, and they are full of honor. Only in this case can there be a Stakhanovite movement. This is very obvious.

"The third source of the Stakhanovite movement is the existence of new technologies in our country. The Stakhanovite movement has been inextricably linked to new technologies from the beginning. Without new technologies, without new factories and new machines, the Stakhanovite movement could not have occurred in our country. Without new technologies, the technical level can only be increased by one or two times, not more. If the technical level increases five or six times, it means that they are completely built on new technologies. It means that our country's industrialization, the transformation of our country's factories, and the existence of new technologies and new machines have opened up a road for the Stakhanovite movement." But only new technologies cannot make us progress so much. Even if there are first-class technologies, even if there are first-class factories, but no one can surpass this kind of technology, technology is only technology. In order for new technologies to produce their effect, there must be powerful people, cadres, and working men and women who can dominate technology and promote technology.

"The emergence and development of the Stakhanovite movement indicates that such cadres have risen among our working men and women. Two years ago, the Party said that although we have new factories, although we have new machines for various gold industries, our work is only half completed. The Party said that the enthusiasm for building new factories must be supplemented by the enthusiasm for dominating new factories. Only in this way can we achieve great success. In these two years, the work of dominating new machines and cultivating new cadres has obviously been carried out, and it is clear that we now have such cadres. Without these new people, we would not have any Stakhanovite movement. This is very easy to understand. Therefore, the new people from working men and women who are able to dominate new technologies have formed a force to generate and promote the Stakhanovite movement.

"I said that the Stakhanovite movement did not develop gradually, but like the bursting of a dike. Obviously, it has overcome various obstacles. Some people have blocked it, some people have troubled it, but now the Stakhanovite movement has accumulated strength, broke through obstacles, and flooded the country. What does this mean? Who is the real obstacle to this kind of movement? This is the old technical level, and the people who protect this kind of level. "Several years ago, our engineers, technicians, and economic workers adapted to the technologically backward working men and women and established a certain technical level. Since then, several years have passed. During this period, the people have gradually developed and obtained a technical foundation, but the technical level has not changed. This level has become an obstacle to our new people. This is very obvious. Can we still be loyal to our backwardness? Can we take the permanent backwardness of our working men and women as a starting point? We seem to have failed to move further from this question. Why? Perhaps because we do not have enough courage to break the conservatism of our engineers and technicians, break the old traditions and standards, so that the revolutionary forces of the laboring class can be fully developed. What else?

"They talk about science. It is said that some books on technical materials issue orders against the demands of the Stakhanovite movement to improve technical standards. But what is meant by science here? Scientific materials are often hindered by practice and experience. What kind of science is capable of breaking the connection between it and practice and experience? Science is called science precisely because it can deny inherited ideas, not be afraid to raise its hand to resist the past that is trending towards death, and listen to the voices of experience and practice. "If it were not for this, we would not have any science. Take astronomy as an example, we will adhere to Ptolemy's outdated theoretical system. We will have no biology and still seek comfort in human creation legends. We will have no chemistry and still adhere to the prophecies of alchemists. This is why I often think that our engineering, technical, and economic workers are always far behind the Stakhanovite movement. They must abandon their old technical standards and place themselves on the Stakhanovite road to succeed. Or will ask me, in general, how should technical standards be reformed? Or said that we do not need any technical standards. This is also wrong. And it is stupid. "Without technical standards, planned economy will be impossible. In addition, technical standards are also necessary to promote the backward masses and make them catch up with the level of advanced workers. Technical standards are a great regulatory force that can organize the labor masses in industry around the leading members of the laboring class. Therefore, we need technical standards, but not the existing standards, but higher standards.

"Some people also say that technical standards are still necessary; but they must be increased to the levels reached by Stakhanovs, Busyginss, and Vinogradovss. This is also wrong. This kind of standard is not possible at present; because the less technologically advanced working men and women will not be able to complete this kind of standard. The technical standards we need are between the existing standards and the standards of Stakhanov and others. "In any case, one thing is very clear, that is, the existing technical standards are not in line with the facts. They are backward and have become an obstacle to our industry; in order to prevent the development of industry from being hindered, they must be replaced by new and higher technical standards. New people, new era, new technical standards.

"From the point of view of the benefits of the Stakhanovite movement, what will be our future tasks? First, our task is to help the movement of Stakhanovite movers, so that it continues to develop, so that it is popularized and deeply rooted in various provinces and regions of the Soviet Union. On the other hand, we must eliminate the various stubborn conservatives among the economic, engineering, and technical workers, who are unwilling to move forward and systematically obstruct the Stakhanovite movement. "I believe that if we can complete this kind of work, the Stakhanovite movement will be able to fully develop, will be able to encompass the whole country, and show us the miracle of new achievements.

"A few more words need to be said to explain this conference and its significance. Lenin said that a true leader, a Bolshevik Party member, must be someone who not only teaches workers, but also learns from workers and peasants. Some party members are unwilling to accept Lenin's words. But history shows that Lenin is 100% correct in this. Millions of workers and peasants are indeed working, living, and fighting. Who can say that they are living in blind life and not accumulating huge experience in life and struggle? Who can doubt that a leader who ignores this kind of experience will not become a leader? Therefore, our Party and government leaders must not only teach laborers, but also learn from them. I do not deny that you have received some education from government leaders by attending this conference, and at the same time, our government leaders have also received a lot of education from you Stakhanovite movers. Comrades, thank you, thank you for the lessons you have given me." (Thunderous applause) (TASS Telegram of the 22nd)

"China Clipper" Begins Trans-Pacific Airmail Service

Direct Flight from San Francisco to Manila, U.S. Postmaster General Attends Launching Ceremony

San Francisco Postmaster General Farley arrived here today to attend tomorrow's launching ceremony of the giant "China Clipper" flying boat, which will officially carry airmail tomorrow, flying to Honolulu, Midway Island, Wake Island, Guam, and finally Manila. Mr. Farley will be the main speaker at a grand celebration at the Alameda Airport tomorrow. After the speech, the plane will take off carrying letters from stamp collectors and 6,000 other letters. Other speakers will include California Governor Merriam and San Francisco Mayor Rossi. Philippine Commonwealth President Quezon and Hawaii Governor Poindexter will broadcast speeches to congratulate the conference here. The plane will carry letters from Mayor Rossi to Governor Poindexter, President Quezon, and Governor George, inviting them to participate in the 1938 San Francisco World's Fair. (National Telegram of the 21st)

Miami The "Philippine Clipper," a sister ship to America's largest plane, the "China Clipper," will leave here on Friday for San Francisco to prepare to carry mail across the Pacific. The plane, piloted by Dusturd, will spend the night in Acapulco, Mexico, and then fly to San Francisco via San Diego and Los Angeles along the route taken by the "China Clipper." US Airways officials said the "Philippine Clipper" had a successful test flight in the Caribbean. (National Telegram of the 21st)

Oakland Representatives of both the New Zealand government and Pan American Airways will sign a contract here tomorrow to conduct trans-Pacific air services, with Oakland as the terminal. French North Africa to Build Naval Base to Control the Western Mediterranean

(Paris) Naval Minister Pietri recently decided to build a new naval base on the coast of French Algeria in Africa. The Petit Parisien newspaper commented on this today, saying that this decision is extremely important. The new naval base is built in the port of Mers El Kébir near the city of Oran, which is backed by mountains and faces the sea, with a dangerous terrain. It is also an essential route to the Strait of Gibraltar. After the construction of the naval base is completed, the French Navy can control the western Mediterranean. France lacks seaplane bases on the northern coast of the Mediterranean Sea, which can be remedied. In addition, an underground tunnel will be built between the port of Mers El Kébir and the city of Oran. (Central News Agency Telegram of the 22nd)

American Military Officer Creates Record By Ascending Into the Stratosphere in a Balloon

Reached an Altitude of Over 72,000 Feet, Officially Announced by the National Aeronautic Association

(Washington) The National Aeronautic Association announced today that the stratospheric balloon "Explorer II" reached an altitude of 72,395 feet on November 11 after taking off in Tancy City. This is the highest record, as the previous record of the Soviet Union was 68,892 feet. This time, the "Explorer II" ascended to the stratosphere for inspection, initiated by the National Geographic Society and the U.S. Army Air Corps. This world's largest balloon fell into White Lake in the sky for about eight hours, 230 miles from the starting point. (Reuters Telegram of the 21st)

While their significance should not be underestimated, they should also not be overemphasized. At present, the European situation is quite serious, and all countries are most anxious. British and French Experts Confer on Methods for Italian-Ethiopian Reconciliation; 600 Ethiopian Soldiers Defend Peak Against Enemy

(Paris) After arriving here from London yesterday, the British Foreign Office's expert on Ethiopian affairs, Mr. Patteson, will meet with the Director of African Affairs of the French Foreign Ministry, Mr. Saint-Quentin, to seek a new basis for a friendly solution to the Italo-Ethiopian conflict. The League of Nations General Assembly's Committee on Adjustments to the Sanctions Plan previously adopted the proposal of Belgian Prime Minister de Broqueville, entrusting Britain and France with finding a way to end the Italo-Ethiopian war. The meeting between Patteson and Saint-Quentin is to fulfill this mission. (Havas, 22nd)

Magal, Tigray - General Seyoum, west of Tigray, has been avoiding contact with Italian columns. Today, he finally clashed with the 15th battalion of the Italian indigenous army at Danbyan with 600 men. These 600 men were positioned on a mountain peak 6,000-7,000 feet high, using the famous Amba Aradam fortress as a shield, and bombarded the Italian soldiers with rifles and machine guns for several hours. Seeing Italian reinforcements arrive, they retreated into the mountains. The Italians claim that they suffered few casualties in the battle.

King Haile Selassie took advantage of this opportunity to travel to Jijiga for a military conference with General Nasibu, commander of the southern Ethiopian army, and General Welde Tsadiq. He has decided on a new Ethiopian military strategy. This was the first time the King had traveled by airplane, which can be considered a break with tradition. According to eyewitnesses, the trip was very effective. He was greeted with thunderous cheers wherever he went. Upon arriving in Jijiga, he reviewed the troops and exhorted the soldiers to fight cautiously. He also went to the Swedish hospital to award medals to several wounded soldiers. He then traveled by car from Jijiga to Dagabur, where he was very interested to see four light tankette vehicles seized by Ethiopian troops from the enemy near Anale. He then returned to the capital by plane, arriving safely this morning. When departing from Harar, he narrowly escaped an attack by two Italian planes. (Reuters, 21st)

Ethiopian Emperor Returns to Capital, Says Military Strength Sufficient to Resist Powerful Enemy; Aircraft Effectiveness Very Limited

After returning to the capital from the front lines, the Ethiopian Emperor was interviewed in writing by a special correspondent of the Associated Press. According to the Emperor's reply, "Up to now, the fighting strength of the southern army has proven sufficient to resist modern armies and even defeat them." He also said, "The Italian army has not fully achieved its objectives and has fabricated many false victories. The Italian planes have not been able to threaten our generals, soldiers, and civilians. Their bombing effectiveness is very limited. For example, in the Golahei area, Italian planes dropped 100 bombs, resulting in only 17 deaths and injuries." (National News Agency, 22nd)

Addis Ababa - After inspecting the southern front lines, the Emperor returned to the capital. It is said that there are many reasons to ensure the solidity of the Ethiopian army's positions. The Emperor denied Italian claims of a major victory in the Ogaden province and the defection of Ethiopian chieftains to the Italian army. He also said that although Italian planes launched aerial attacks, the Ethiopian people remained calm. The Emperor's entourage reiterated the story of the Ethiopian army capturing four Italian tanks, as witnessed that day. According to the account, six men in the vehicles were killed on the spot, one escaped in a motorized vehicle, and the remaining one hid inside the vehicle, resisting arrest with a gun. An Ethiopian soldier, wounded in one eye, angrily extended his arm into the viewing hole, grabbed the man's hair, and dragged his head out of the hole, severing his head from his body with a sharp knife. The Ethiopian army now has four vehicles and is scrambling for the hand grenades inside. Due to carelessness, one grenade fell to the ground and exploded, killing one comrade and injuring two others. (Reuters, 21st)

Jijiga - Because the Emperor personally came to the front line yesterday, morale has been greatly boosted. Today, the army launched a counter-offensive against the Italian army south of Dagabur. Despite Italian aerial bombardment, they were able to intercept four tanks and capture many prisoners. (National News Agency, 21st)

Addis Ababa - According to a public bulletin here, an Italian unit departed from Magal and advanced northwest, entering an area ambushed by the Ethiopian army. The Ethiopian soldiers all leaped out from their hiding places behind rocks and trees and opened fire on the enemy soldiers. This was followed by hand-to-hand combat. The enemy suffered heavy losses, their commander was killed, and several soldiers died. The remaining troops fled back to Magal. (Reuters, 22nd)

Asmara - Staff officers of the Italian army here are confident that the Italian army will be able to hold the territory it has occupied on the northern front. Although aerial reconnaissance reports that at least 50,000 Ethiopian soldiers have gathered south of Magal, Italian authorities say that if the Ethiopian army attacks, it will be heavily bombarded by the artillery units currently stationed at Magal. (Reuters, 22nd)

Asmara - The headquarters here announced today that white soldiers fighting on behalf of Ethiopia cannot expect leniency from the Italian army. It is known that there are many foreigners in Ethiopia currently leading the Ethiopian army to fight against Italy. (National News Agency, 21st)

Mediterranean Sea: British Naval Maneuvers of Unprecedented Scale

Alexandria - The British Navy held combat exercises in the eastern Mediterranean Sea today. The scale of the exercises was unprecedented in the Mediterranean. When Prince Muhammad Ali, nephew of the King of Egypt, boarded the British cruiser HMS Berwick to observe the exercises, a 21-gun salute was fired. He was accompanied by the Egyptian Prime Minister, his cabinet members, and Sir Miles Lampson, the British High Commissioner for Egypt and Sudan. A division of warships, including five battleships, six cruisers, eighteen destroyers, and two aircraft carriers, led by the cruiser HMS Ajax, advanced in a line. The five battleships fired 21 rounds each from their 15-inch guns at a target 11 miles away, causing it to break into two pieces. Destroyers provided smoke screen cover and participated in the attack. Sixty aircraft practiced dropping bombs. (Reuters, 21st)

US Oil Shipments to Italy Halted: Interior Secretary Tells Merchants to Comply Voluntarily

(Washington) The Secretary of the Interior and Administrator of the Federal Oil Administration, Ickes, today requested that all crude oil producers in the country assist the government in stopping sales to belligerent nations to avoid war. (National News Agency, 21st)

(Washington) Interior Secretary Ickes asked the American oil industry to voluntarily stop shipping oil to Italy. Ickes issued a statement today saying that the Bureau of Mines' report showed that oil shipments to Italy in September were higher than in August. Although he has no authority over the matter, he feels that oil companies should understand the government's efforts to prevent the supply of war materials to belligerent countries. (Reuters, 21st)

Houston - Southern oil companies have expressed their willingness to comply with Interior Secretary Ickes' advice to oil companies to voluntarily stop shipping oil to Italy. Officials at Standard Oil of New Jersey stated that the company had already stopped selling oil to Italy weeks ago. Shell Oil also stated that it had not shipped any oil abroad. Mexican Oil and other companies also said that they must comply with government warnings. (Reuters, 22nd)

(London) After the U.S. government advised its oil companies not to ship oil to Italy, political and oil industry circles here are very pleased, especially political circles, which believe that the U.S. government's attitude towards sanctions against Italy is in line with that of other countries, especially Britain. This will definitely benefit the negotiations between the British and American oil industries, and the views of the U.S. and the League of Nations on this matter will become more aligned. Previously, the British oil industry was deeply concerned that after the League of Nations member states imposed an oil embargo on Italy, the U.S. might profit from it. Now that concern has been alleviated, but it is said that the reaction of the American oil industry still needs to be observed. (Havas, 22nd)

(Geneva) Since the member states of the League of Nations implemented sanctions against Italy, the League of Nations itself has also implemented sanctions. Going forward, the Secretariat of the League of Nations will try to avoid purchasing Italian goods. For example, the materials used to build the new League of Nations headquarters and other supplies will no longer be purchased from Italy. The Secretariat of the League of Nations also has a bar, originally opened by an Italian citizen. The League of Nations is now also requiring the owner of the bar to stop purchasing Italian goods. (Havas, 22nd)

(Rome) The United Federation of Fruit and Vegetable Growers held a meeting yesterday to study the impact of the sanctions implemented by the member states of the League of Nations on the industry and to discuss appropriate countermeasures. Prime Minister Mussolini personally chaired the meeting. Italy's annual production of fruits and vegetables ranges from 6.7 million to 8 million metric tons, second only to grain in terms of production volume. Most of those who buy fresh fruits and vegetables from Italy are countries that do not participate in the sanctions, while the number purchased by countries participating in the sanctions is relatively small. Therefore, after the implementation of sanctions, this export commodity should not be significantly affected. As for citrus fruits, this year's harvest is not very abundant, so even if it is sanctioned, it is not a major concern. On the other hand, the sale of lemons, which are subject to sanctions, will be severely affected, but the quantity sold in the domestic market is still considerable, so there is no need to worry. In addition, Italy relies heavily on foreign countries for dried vegetables. Although the source of supply will be cut off in the future, domestic production can still be increased. However, canned fruits and vegetables will be greatly affected, as the annual production value of these commodities is in the range of 50,000 lire, half of which is exported to foreign countries, and there will be no way out in the future. However, the Federation has decided to make efforts to expand domestic consumption to remedy the situation and advocates the establishment of a joint operation company for all of the above commodities for centralized management. (Havas, 22nd)

Political Turmoil Brewing in France: Laval's Enigmatic Financial and Diplomatic Policies; Determined to Fight the Socialist Party with All His Might; National Bank's Reserves Decreasing

(Paris) When the Chamber of Deputies meets next week, the Socialist Party is determined to launch a vigorous attack on the government. Therefore, France is now in danger of seeing another cabinet crisis. According to political observers, since the Socialist Party has made this decision, Prime Minister Laval's chances of coping with the political and financial turmoil will be greatly reduced. The Socialist Party will use the issue of the fascist associations as a way to attack. The left-wing parties have been increasingly opposed to these associations, especially because of the shooting incident in Limoges on November 16, which injured 33 people. The Socialist Party and the Communist Party are now demanding the suppression of these associations, one of the main ones being organized by veterans. The members of the Radical Party hold divergent opinions. Their representative in the government, led by Herriot, believes that because the diplomatic situation is currently tense, and the franc's position is very unstable, they oppose triggering a cabinet crisis at this time. However, the extreme left-wing, led by former Prime Minister Daladier, is eager to overthrow Laval. The tense situation is actually caused by the interplay of politics and finance. Due to the political unrest, gold has been flowing out of the Bank of France's treasury. Laval will probably fight to the death in the Chamber of Deputies to fight the Socialist Party, not only to preserve his position, but also to maintain the franc and maintain the continuity of French foreign policy. Laval may rely on the unstable position of the franc to make the Radical Party fearful and turn to him for assistance. (Reuters, 22nd)

(Paris) According to the Bank of France's weekly report (from November 8 to November 15), the gold outflow totaled 933,000,000 francs, and reserves decreased to 70,398,000,000 francs. The discount rate increased by 298,000,000 francs, reaching 8,121,000,000 francs. Short-term loans secured by government bonds increased by more than 40 million francs. As for the bank's liabilities, the amount of banknotes in circulation decreased by 644,000,000 francs, and long-term deposits and demand deposits increased by a total of 227,000,000 francs. The reserve ratio decreased from 74.40 percent to 73.82 percent. (Havas, 21st)

(Paris) The Bank of France today increased the discount rate again from 4 percent to 5 percent. This action is the second in a week. On November 14, the discount rate suddenly increased from 3 percent to 4 percent. It is said that the reason is to stop the outflow of large amounts of cash, and it also reflects the domestic political unrest. Currently, advocates of inflation are becoming more active, and the movement advocating the devaluation of the franc is also visibly increasing. (National News Agency, 21st)

National Foreign Trade Convention of the U.S.: Concludes, Issues Declaration, Advocates Repeal of Silver Purchase Act, Permanent Restoration of Gold Standard

Houston - The National Foreign Trade Convention, held here, concluded today and issued a formal declaration stating the association's views on banking, commerce, government policies, and matters related to the revival of world trade, advocating the following three things: (1) Permanent restoration of the gold standard; (2) Balancing the budget; (3) Restoring sound foreign lending, as the primary business of a creditor nation. The declaration advocates the repeal of the Silver Purchase Act and opposes methods to limit agricultural production. As for trade between Japan and the U.S., it advocates maintaining it. In addition, the declaration also supports government subsidies for the construction of merchant ships and reciprocal trade agreements, but condemns national self-sufficiency or bilateral trade balance as absurd. (Reuters, 21st)

(New York) "Literary Digest" magazine solicited opinions from the people of the country on the New Deal. The first batch of answers has already been published today. The magazine's question was "Do you now agree with all the measures and policies of President Roosevelt's New Deal to date?" In total, 53.28 percent of the earliest answers expressed opposition. The magazine announced that the first batch of answers received totaled 40,053, representing the five states of Virginia and Oklahoma, with a majority in favor. The three states of Iowa, Kansas, and Missouri, however, were mostly opposed. However, its editorial staff said today that it is too early to determine the outcome. The magazine's "voting test" has always been very accurate, and the difference between the predictions of past elections and the actual results has been only 2 percent at most. (National News Agency, 21st)

Rumors Run Rampant Around Yu and Qin: Japanese Troops Arriving Successively; Residents Relocating One After Another

(Tianjin) The Matsui Brigade troops newly arrived at Shanhaiguan were dispatched to suppress bandits in the vicinity of Suizhong. Today, one trainload of soldiers was dispatched to suppress them. Rumors between Yu and Qin are increasing, and more people are relocating. Although the Public Security Bureau has tried to dissuade them, it has been ineffective. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Tianjin) Rumors in the various towns and cities of eastern Hebei are becoming more and more rampant. The Tangshan Public Security Bureau has dispatched police to patrol at street corners to search pedestrians. Japanese military police stationed in Luan County are also inspecting departing travelers. Several military policemen are permanently stationed at the station. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

(Beijing) A person arriving from Yu Guan stated that the Japanese troops arriving at Yu Guan totaled about a mixed brigade of less than 10,000 men. The Japanese troops at Gubeikou are now being transferred from Luanping to Gubeikou, the number of troops is unknown. Huo Shi, director of the Jiji District Office stationed at Gubeikou, has now left Beijing to return to Gubeikou. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

After the Matsui and other units of the Japanese army stationed in Jinzhou and Suizhong concentrated at Yu Guan and the various passes of the Great Wall, rumors started in Qinhuangdao and Yu Guan. Although there are many warships of various countries in the waters off Yu Guan, there are no abnormalities, so the local situation is still considered calm. However, people are panicked, stores close early, pedestrians are few, and wealthy households are mostly moving elsewhere, causing the market in Lin Yu to be quite deserted. Rumors have recently started again in Tangshan, and grain prices have risen. Local authorities have begun to impose martial law, and people are extremely panicked. Wealthy households in Tangshan are mostly moving to Beijing, Tianjin, and other places with their families. The Tangshan Public Security Bureau has dispatched personnel to inspect brothels, hotels, and entertainment venues within the territory. Rumors have been rampant in Luan County recently. The Japanese military police team stationed in Luan County, to prevent burglars from sneaking into the county seat, has dispatched 10 police officers to the station starting on the 22nd of this month to inspect passengers coming and going. Planned Sino-Japanese Trade Association

(Tianjin) The Sino-Japanese Trade Association, initiated by industrial and economic circles of China and Japan, is scheduled to be established on the 5th of next month. The headquarters will be established in Tokyo, a general headquarters in Shanghai, and branch offices in major ports. A regular meeting will be convened once a year, with the location rotating. One chairman will be set up in the Tokyo and Shanghai headquarters, to be elected by the managing directors. The chairman of the Tokyo headquarters will be Japanese, and the chairman of the Shanghai general headquarters will be Chinese. Two managing vice-chairmen will be appointed, one of Chinese nationality and one of Japanese nationality. Wu Dingchang is expected to be the Chinese chairman, and Kodama Kenji is determined to be the Japanese chairman. (Special Dispatch, 22nd)

Measures for Civil Servants to Subscribe to Disaster Relief Bonds; Percentage Determined After Review by the Executive Yuan

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan convened a review meeting on the morning of the 22nd, bringing together various ministries and commissions, including the Ministry of Interior, Ministry of Finance, Ministry of Economic Affairs, and the National Relief Commission. They reviewed the measures for civil servants to subscribe to public bonds for flood relief and work relief, and the review has been completed. The regulations specify the subscription percentages: civil servants in central government agencies and provincial/municipal governments with a monthly salary of 200 yuan or more will subscribe 10 yuan; those with 300 yuan or more will subscribe 20 yuan; those with 400 yuan or more will subscribe 30 yuan; and those with 500 yuan or more will subscribe 40 yuan. The duration is limited to two months, starting from January 1, 1936. Opinions will be drafted within the next few days and submitted to the President of the Executive Yuan for approval, after which they will be presented to the Executive Yuan meeting for discussion and approval. International Commercial Telegram – Special Commercial Intelligence Telegram from Reuters, November 22nd

Gold and Silver

London: The gold price today was 141 shillings and 3 pence, down 2 pence.

London: The silver market was quiet today. Prices fell by 0.0625 due to the weak dollar. The spot price was 29 pence and 25, and the futures price was 28 pence and 9375. The United States purchased, and India sold. Closing sentiment was stable.

Exchange Rates

United States/England: The London foreign exchange market was stable today. The US/UK exchange rate for the pound was slightly weak, opening at $4.93375, up 0.025 from yesterday's US/UK closing price. It rose 0.01875 within the first hour to $4.935625, fell 0.0125 at noon, and continued to fall 0.00625 at 2 pm to $4.93375. The British/French franc was initially weak but stabilized after adjustments by the Exchange Equalisation Account. The opening price was 75 francs 03, up 10 points, but it shrank 6 points within the first hour and continued to fall 6 points at noon to 74 francs 91, after which there were no changes.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: Opening prices this morning were largely unchanged. There was a reactive trend before noon due to falling Liverpool cotton prices and renewed profit-taking in the domestic market. It is rumored that the US cotton reserve agency may sell January cotton without replenishing the distant months. It is expected that the government will take some action to prevent squeezes. There is also talk in the cotton market of a possible port workers' strike.

Liverpool Cotton: Prices were stable today but with a slight downward trend. At 1 pm, the January price was 6.51, down 2 points.

Chicago Wheat: The opening price rose 0.75 due to the sharp rise in Liverpool prices this morning. However, the opening price could hardly be maintained afterward. Feed grains opened slightly higher but then fell.

Liverpool Wheat: Today, due to good overseas telegrams and the fact that southern wheat exports were beneficial to the bulls, the opening was firm. Although there was some profit-taking afterward, prices rose rapidly due to renewed buying. At 1 pm, the December contract rose 1.25 pence to 6 shillings, 2 pence and 375.

Rubber

London: The opening today was stable. The January/March price was 6 pence and 3125, unchanged. Trading was quiet before noon. The price was unchanged at noon. New York opened slightly lower today but then rose. The market continued to be panic-stricken, fearing that the Restriction Committee would increase the quota for the Dutch East Indies. At the same time, the weakness of the Dutch currency was also a reason for market instability.

Securities

New York: The opening this morning was firm. Continued purchases from Europe boosted sentiment. Utility stocks remained firm, especially New York Gas. Mining stocks also showed improvement due to profit reports. Department store stocks rose slightly due to rising wheat prices. The later market was slightly mixed. Steel stocks fell below yesterday's closing price. The Dow Jones average of 30 industrial stocks opened at 147.58, up 21 points. The New York stock market prices are listed below:

Northeast Gold Mines: Japanese and Puppet Regime Actively Develop

This year, no less than 10 million yuan; future trends will continue to increase

Changchun Newsletter: The gold production in Northeast China has always been a focus of world attention. The following is a summary of information from various Japanese and puppet regime sources. According to the Japanese side, the amount of gold produced in Northeast China this year is estimated to be absolutely no less than 10 million yuan. For example, the "Manchuria" Gold Mining Company's performance from January to August this year yielded 1.81 million yuan, with 600,000 yuan in August alone. From August to December, the average monthly yield should be 500,000 yuan. Other gold mining companies are reported to have earned 3.6 million yuan. Furthermore, there are more than 15,000 employees in the gold mining industry in Northeast China. Therefore, it is quite reliable to estimate that the actual yield will be within 7.5 million yuan based on previous harvests. Even if we use a general statistical estimate, it is certain that it will be 10 million yuan. Moreover, the estimated purchase of gold produced from January to August exceeded 6 million yuan. Therefore, the aforementioned amount of gold produced can be largely believed. With the active management of the Japanese, the amount of gold produced in Northeast China will continue to increase.

Songjiang

Villagers Vaguely Report Kidnapping Case

Yu Fugen, a villager from two households in the fourth Jia of the seventh Bao of the Caoging Hutang Township, was suddenly attacked by armed bandits on the evening of the 7th of this month. His wife, Yu Shen, and his sister, A Mian, were kidnapped. Before leaving, they also stole tablecloths, fabrics, and other items and fired a shot to demonstrate their power. Yu Fugen immediately reported the kidnapping and robbery to the Eighth District Office, which forwarded the report to the county government, which in turn ordered the Ninth Sub-station of the Public Security Bureau to investigate. The report has now been submitted to the county government, stating that Yu is a poor man, so why would he attract the attention of bandits? After a detailed investigation, it was said that his sister had previously been involved with a robbery leader named Li. Li is currently hiding in Shanghai to avoid the authorities, so he sent his followers to the village to take his mistress away to live with him. It is said that this information is more plausible.

Suzhou

Money Shop Reserve Bank Established

The Wuxian Money Shop Association, in view of the recent series of closures of money shops in Suzhou due to runs on deposits, decided to establish a Wuxian Money Shop Reserve Bank after Yuankang collapsed and Jiufeng Tiansheng successively announced their suspension of operations. Considering this concerns the entire financial situation, they repeatedly held meetings to discuss ways to stabilize Suzhou's financial market. It has been unanimously decided to establish the Wuxian Money Shop Reserve Bank, with a reserve fund of 500,000 yuan. Each money shop will invest according to the amount of its capital. Xu Hancheng was elected as the director of the reserve bank, and Huang Ruijun, Zhu Zijing, Yin Junren, and Zheng Fanwu were elected as accountants and clerks. The reserve bank has been formally established. In the future, if any of the fellow businesses experience a run on deposits, the reserve bank will provide as much assistance as possible in the spirit of mutual assistance among fellow businesses.

Nantong

Special Commissioner's Office Punishes Police Officers Who Protect Gambling

The Nantong District Administrative Inspector's Office has determined that Du Mingzai, the Director of the First Branch of the Rugao Public Security Bureau, Xie Yun, the Chief of the Qidong Public Security Section, and Patrol Officer Liu Shoutian, among others, have been protecting gambling activities. Orders have been issued to dismiss and punish them.

Hangzhou

Qiantang River South Bank Dam Completed

The No. 104 training dike on the south bank of the Qiantang River was destroyed by huge waves due to the exceptionally large autumn tides this year. Considering the dike's significant impact on the safety of the South Bank Ferry Terminal and the highway and railway, the Water Conservancy Bureau applied to the Construction Department for funds to repair it under the work relief project. After two months of construction, it has now been completely completed. A special request has been made to the Construction Department to send personnel to inspect and accept it. There is no longer any danger to the riverbank wharf, the Xiao-Shao Highway, and the Hang-Jiang Railway.

Yuan Kewen, the fourth son of Yuan Shikai, who was arrested in Ningbo for being destitute and addicted to drugs, was transferred by the Ningbo Public Security Bureau to the Yin County District Court at 2 pm on the 20th. Chief Prosecutor Gao then opened a court hearing and ordered him to be released on bail. Because Yuan is unfamiliar with the area and has no guarantor to find, he is currently being held in the detention center.

Local News

Shanghai Business Community Petitions Government to Rescue Industries; Proposes Establishing Special Financial Institutions or Allocating Large Sums from the Three Banks

Shanghai business leaders Yu Hesui, Rong Zongjing, Liu Hongsheng, Guo Shun, Nie Lusheng, and others yesterday separately submitted petitions to Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei, Legislative Yuan President Sun Ke, Military Affairs Commission Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, National Economic Commission Standing Committee Member Song Ziwen, Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi, and Industry Minister Chen Gongbo, requesting the government to rescue industries. Excerpts from the original text are as follows: "Regarding the petition, we believe that in recent years, financial resources have been scarce, silver has flowed out, all industries have declined, and production has decreased daily. If we continue without providing relief, the total economic collapse will become almost inevitable. Fortunately, the government resolutely reformed the currency policy and implemented managed currency. On the day the order was issued, the entire country responded positively. Although implementation has just begun, financial activities have been seen in the market, and international exchange rates have gradually stabilized. Friendly countries have provided support, and the people have embraced it. It cannot be said that this is not a good plan for governing the country and a great strategy for saving the times. However, various industries, which are the foundation of the nation's economic life, are still on the verge of collapse due to a lack of working capital, and production is decreasing daily, resulting in a daily increase in imports over exports. We have not yet received assistance from the government. If we continue to allow industrialists to seek their own solutions, begging at the doors of banks as before, then most of our domestic banks are commercial organizations and are unable to engage in industrial lending due to insufficient capital. Moreover, even if they are slightly accommodating, they mostly require guarantees of the products produced and are unwilling to accept loans on real estate. Under these circumstances, not only are entrepreneurs in a difficult situation, but also a significant amount of capital is invisibly reduced in society, how can production not decline, and how can imports not increase sharply? Following this result, how can the reformed currency policy not be shaken? Therefore, to save the industries to save the country, now is the time when the government's financial resources are concentrated and credit has been established. It is urgently necessary to establish special financial institutions, with the government in charge, roughly imitating the industrial, development, or promotion bank systems of various countries, specializing in rescuing industries, and using the fixed assets owned by industrialists as collateral for loans, with long-term, low-interest rates to meet their needs. On the one hand, the Central Bank should lower market interest rates and find ways to recover high-interest bonds so that funds are not concentrated on bonds alone. In this way, domestic businesses can have a turnaround, and international trade can be balanced. Otherwise, if production does not improve, even if the government suspends convertibility to balance exchange rates, imports will still be imports, what good will it do? Moreover, because industries are declining, unemployment will increase, society will become more difficult to stabilize, national tax revenues will become shorter, and the future of the nation's foundation will become more dangerous. Some say that this move by the government is a strategy to concentrate strength and unify finance, and that the issuance of currency should still have a statutory reserve to secure the government's credit. If currency is issued to fill capital without a reserve, it is tantamount to inflating the currency, which will inevitably lead to currency depreciation and rising prices. They do not know that the issuance and withdrawal of currency must be based on the supply and demand of the market. If currency is issued for production, then the currency is the capital of the production industry, and the assets of the production industry are the indirect reserve for the issuance. The currency value will naturally not depreciate. There are clear precedents in European and American countries. Moreover, in the future, as production increases, national tax revenues will also increase as a result. Why would the government not be happy to do something that benefits in several ways with one action? Now, the essence is summarized into two points: 1. Please establish a special bank as soon as possible, or first allocate a large sum from the Central Bank of China and the Bank of Communications to rescue the industry, so that various businessmen can fully utilize all their capital. 2. Please the Central Bank reduce market interest rates and find ways to recover high-interest bonds to encourage the general public to invest in industry. The situation is critical, and we urgently hope that you will implement it. If we miss the opportunity, I am afraid that it will be too late to save. Therefore, we do not hesitate to offend and respectfully appeal to your seat to consider that industry is related to the foundation of the country, and to quickly approve the implementation. Then the dying industry will hopefully obtain a chance of survival. The industry and commerce are fortunate, and the country is fortunate. Respectfully presented."

President Wang Went to the Hospital for Medical Treatment Yesterday; X-Ray Examination Revealed a Bullet Remaining on the Right Side of the Spine; Determined the Correct Location and Not Necessary to Remove

Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday for quiet recuperation. Besides previously inviting the Niu Huilin brothers and Doctors Noel on the morning before, the only issue that needs to be studied regarding President Wang's injury is whether the bullet in his back needs to be removed, which is still questionable. Therefore, President Wang again invited Dr. Niu Huisheng and Dr. Noel at 8:00 am yesterday morning, accompanied by Madam Chen Bijun, Vice Minister of Railways Zeng Zhongming, and others, and took his own car from his private residence on Anhe Temple Road to the Hongen Hospital on Great West Road, where he borrowed the hospital's X-ray machine for irradiation. It took about an hour. President Wang then returned to his residence to recuperate. Afterwards, Dr. Niu Huisheng visited President Wang's residence to report at around 10:00 am, and then visited twice more at around 5:00 pm and 9:00 pm last night. According to Dr. Niu's conversation with the reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency last night, the bullet in President Wang's back was previously X-rayed at the Central Hospital, but the photos were not very clear due to mechanical reasons, and the exact location could not be found. Having borrowed the Hongen Hospital's X-ray machine for irradiation this morning (i.e., yesterday morning), the correct location of the bullet has been determined. It is located on the right side of the fifth section of the spine, about an inch away from the spine and about one and a half inches deep. In my opinion, it is not necessary to remove it. Leaving it in place will not harm his health and can save all sorts of trouble. It is feared that after the operation, fever and other reactions may inevitably occur. There are precedents for not removing bullets such as this in foreign countries. For example, former US President Roosevelt and former French President Clemenceau were both shot and had bullets left in their bodies. The location of their bullets were in the brain, but it did not affect them, and they both enjoyed long lives. Now, the bullet in President Wang's back should be even less of a problem. Some of President Wang's relatives and friends are afraid of future troubles and advise him to have the bullet removed, but I advocate that there is no need to do this. President Wang is in very good spirits, and I have told him that he can stand up and exercise a little, and he will recover completely in a short period of time.

Belgian Minister to China, Mr. and Mrs. Guillaume, traveled south from Peiping on the 15th to preside over the National Modern Art Exhibition held in Nanjing. They then hurriedly came to Shanghai to manage affairs in the Shanghai area. Now that the exhibition is scheduled to close on the 26th, the Belgian Minister took the night express train to Nanjing last night to preside over the closing ceremony. After a short stay, he will return to Shanghai, as the exhibition will be moved to Shanghai after its closing in Nanjing and will be open to the public at the Hamilton House on Sima Road from the 30th. All arrangements are being made by the Belgian Consulate-General in Shanghai, and the minister will personally come to Shanghai to preside over the opening.

Fan Hongxian's Coffin Transported to Nanjing Last Night; Hundreds of People Followed the Hearse; A Plain Carriage and White Horses Displayed Utmost Honor and Mourning

The late General Fan Hongxian, posthumously awarded the rank of Army General, martyred himself for the country twenty years ago. The central government, in order to honor the loyal and righteous, decided through the Central Standing Committee to have him buried in the mausoleum and allocated funeral expenses. A committee was formed to prepare for the burial. Yesterday, the committee, led by Zhang Gongchen and others, escorted the coffin to Nanjing. A public memorial service was held at the North Station at 4:00 PM, and the coffin was transported by the night train, with burial scheduled for January 3rd of next year. Details are as follows:

Transportation to Nanjing for Burial

General Fan was assassinated in Shanghai by Yuan Shikai in the third year of the Republic of China (1914). His coffin was temporarily placed in the Anhui Funeral Home in this city for twenty years. The central government, to honor his loyalty and righteousness, allocated funds for his burial and has surveyed land in the eastern district of the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum to construct a tomb. Construction is nearing completion. The funeral preparation committee dispatched Li Zhengqiu, Zhang Gongchen, and Yin Zhilu as special envoys to Shanghai to retrieve the coffin. The Ministry of Railways specially provided a hearse attached to last night's express train for transport to Nanjing, where it will be temporarily placed in the First Park. The burial is scheduled for January 3rd of next year.

Portrait of the Late General Fan

Funeral Ceremony

The coffin retrieval ceremony was held at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Anhui Funeral Home in Rihui Port. Zhang Gongchen, the special envoy for the retrieval, presided over the ceremony. Representatives from the municipal political party, the military, relatives, and fellow townsmen of the Fan family, totaling over a hundred people, attended the ceremony. The Public Security Bureau's military band played music to express grief. The order of the ceremony was as follows: (1) Music, (2) All stand at attention, (3) Presiding officer takes position, (4) Attendees take position, (5) Dirge, (6) Floral tribute, (7) Reading of the coffin retrieval eulogy, (8) Three bows, (9) One minute of silence, (10) End of silence, (11) Dirge, (12) Ceremony concludes.

Coffin Retrieval Eulogy

Zhang Gongchen, Li Zhengqiu, and Yin Zhilu, Special Envoys of the Funeral Preparation Committee of the Central Executive Committee for the Late General Fan Hongxian, wrote the coffin retrieval eulogy, saying: On this, the twenty-second day of the eleventh month of the twenty-fourth year of the Republic of China, it has been twenty-one years since the late Mr. Fan Fengxian martyred himself for the party. His coffin has been placed in Shanghai, and his final resting place is yet unsettled. Alas! The central government believes that Mr. Fan's meritorious achievements are lofty and that the rites of honoring virtue and rewarding merit must not be neglected. In the seventeenth year [of the Republic], it was decided to establish a funeral preparation committee to bury Mr. Fan in the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum. This year, the national government issued a decree to posthumously commend him and award him the rank of Army General. The funeral preparation committee has selected January 3rd of next year to hold the party funeral. Gongchen, Zhengqiu, Zhilu, and others have come to Shanghai to receive the coffin and will escort it to Nanjing on the twenty-second day of this month and year. On the day of the coffin retrieval, Gongchen, Zhengqiu, Zhilu, and others respectfully prepare fresh flowers and clear wine to offer a tribute to Mr. Fan's coffin and say: Mr. Fan sacrificed himself for the party, and his remains are in Shanghai. For over twenty years, they have been exposed to wild smoke and weeds. Alas! The central government has not forgotten the late martyr and will hold a party funeral for Mr. Fan in the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum on January 3rd of next year. Alas, Mr. Fan, may your spirit come and partake in this offering.

Escorting the Coffin

After the ceremony, the procession escorting the coffin began, stretching for about half a mile. The procession was led by the party and national flags, followed by the Public Security Bureau's band, an honor guard, a float with a portrait of the deceased, the hearse, and hundreds of people from all walks of life following the coffin. The procession departed from the funeral home, passed through Dapu Bridge, and reached Jin Shenfu Road. It then traveled east along Xiafei Road to Baxianqiao, turned north onto Tibet Road, and then turned into Beijing Road, before turning north again onto North Henan Road, finally entering the North Station via Baoshan Road. The local military and police along the route provided strict security. The plain carriage and white horses displayed utmost honor and mourning.

Arrival at the North Station

At the entrance of the North Station, a white cloth banner was hung high. In front of the station, a plain white archway was erected, with the four characters "Spiritual Immortality" written in the middle. On the left and right were elegiac couplets from all the officers and soldiers of the Security Department, which read: "Enlightening the world and guiding the people, leaving a great name to be remembered forever;" "Securing the country and repelling foreign aggression, restoring righteousness and strengthening the mountains and rivers." The special hearse was parked beside the station, and a long table was placed in front of it, with fresh vegetables and fruits offered as a place for public sacrifice. After the coffin arrived at the North Station, it was moved onto the special car by porters. A public memorial service was then held. Fan's only son, Tianjun, and daughter, Xueyun, both of whom had grown up, attended to the coffin with great grief.

Holding a Public Memorial Service

The public memorial service was held at 4:00 PM, presided over by Tong Xingbai, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, Li Dachao, the representative of the Municipal Government, Wang Zhinan, the representative of the Security Department, Li Dasan, the representative of the Railway Party Department, and Xu Shiying. Attendees included representatives from all levels of the municipal party department, representatives from various municipal bureaus, and fellow townsmen of the Fan family, totaling several hundred people. The order was as follows: (1) Music, (2) All stand at attention, (3) Presiding officer takes position, (4) Attendees take position, (5) Dirge, (6) Floral tribute, (7) Reading of the eulogy, (8) Three bows, (9) One minute of silence, (10) End of silence, (11) Dirge, (12) Ceremony concludes. The hearse was attached to the express train and transported to Nanjing at 11:00 PM. The receiving personnel and the Fan family's surviving relatives accompanied the car.

Party and Government Eulogy

On this, the twenty-second day of the eleventh month of the twenty-fourth year of the Republic of China, Wu Tiecheng, Commander of the Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang and concurrently Commander of the Songhu Garrison, and others, respectfully lead representatives from party, government, military, police, and various organizations in offering this sacrifice to the spirit of General Hongxian: Illustrious was Your Excellency, a hero of the Huai and Si regions, born of the mountains and blessed with the essence of the Marquis of Zan. Generous and passionate, taking up arms in simple clothing, You first took up the pen, and your words resonated far and wide. When the Wuchang Uprising erupted, the entire court was shaken. You advised your commander, leading the uprising in Nanjing. Fighting battle after battle, You finally captured the famous city. The captive generals fled, illuminating our banners. With the Central Plains yet to be settled, You vowed to request an expedition, gathering heroes and crossing the iron and blood. But great assistance was not gathered, and You succeeded in haste. Releasing Your sword, You sighed and retreated. The righteous clan rose again, fighting northward. The rebellious generals routed the army, fleeing east to Pengying. Like a fierce tiger crossing the river, none dared to provoke. Ordered to Shenjiang, Your blood boiled with passion. Before the opportunity arose, the mountain collapsed. Like Chen and Song before, Your fervor was comparable to that of Lai and Cen. The party and the nation mourned, and comrades swallowed their grief. With Your death, the nation was weakened; with Your passing, Your name was revered. The nation remembers Your outstanding achievements and has established a new tomb. Your soul will rest in the mausoleum, and Zhongfu will stand tall. For thousands and millions of years, Your heroic spirit will be eternally honored. Incense, flowers, wine, and libations are offered in tribute. Alas! May you accept this sacrifice.

Biography of the Fan Family

The late General Fan Hongxian, named Guangqi, with the pseudonym Guhong, was from Hefei, Anhui. He loved learning from a young age and was known in his hometown for his refined writing style. His family was poor, and he worked diligently, but he never tired of learning. He studied the classics with dedication, became a renowned scholar, and was respected by great scholars across the country. At the age of twenty-eight, he traveled to Shanghai and was invited by Yu Youren to work for the Minhu Bao newspaper. He wrote articles every day advocating for revolution, and his words were passionate and inspiring. The authorities were greatly alarmed and immediately arrested Yu Youren. Mr. Fan ran barefoot, shouting and trying to rescue him. He sued in the Shanghai Mixed Court, arguing eloquently and fearlessly. Although the newspaper was banned, Mr. Yu was able to pay a ransom and be released. From then on, Mr. Fan's name spread far and wide. He, Chen Qimei, and Song Jiaoren were regarded as the leaders of the people's party because of their talents and great integrity. Mr. Fan contributed greatly to the planning and strategy of the Guangzhou Uprising and the Wuchang Uprising. After the righteous army rose, Jiangdong echoed with support. At that time, Xu Shaozhen, the commander of the Qing Dynasty's Ninth Division, led ten thousand elite troops to Nanjing.

Many officers and soldiers wanted to rise up and respond to the Wuchang Uprising, but their plans were not yet decided. Zhang Xun relied on the Jiangfang army and planned to defend firmly, deploying his troops at Yuhuatai and facing the Ninth Division in a strict formation. The generals and officers were fearful and about to collapse. Mr. Fan persuaded Shaozhen, saying: "The Manchu Qing Dynasty is without morals, and the people are disintegrating. Now, the righteous army has risen, and the whole country is responding. This is the time for heaven to destroy them. General, with your wisdom and talent, you are in charge of this important military post. If you seize the opportunity, support righteousness, and conquer, who would dare not follow? By punishing these captives and barbarians and saving China, it is truly a once-in-a-thousand-year opportunity." Shaozhen agreed with his words, ordered his troops to attack Yuhuatai, but they ran out of ammunition and were unable to succeed. After repeated defeats, many soldiers deserted, and they retreated to Zhenjiang. Mr. Fan, along with Lin Shuqing, Bo Wenwei, and Chen Qimei, coordinated and planned, gathered righteous troops, and raised the banner of the Zhejiang-Shanghai Allied Army. They then forcefully attacked Nanjing and captured it. Zhang Xun fled, and Jiangbiao was settled. Mr. Fan's talents were diverse, and his wisdom was destined to change the world. Many heroes from Jianghuai were close to him. Having great ambitions and wanting to distinguish himself in battle, he sought to compete with military heroes. He had long cultivated his roots in Jiang and Wan. At that time, he requested President Sun to recruit five thousand brave men, called the Iron Blood Army, and personally led them. He collected military supplies, trained soldiers, and planned to pacify the Central Plains. When the peace talks were successful, the southern armies were all disbanded. Mr. Fan also assigned the military affairs to Gong Zhenpeng and returned to Shanghai, closing his doors and studying literature and history. People from Wan repeatedly recommended him as the governor of the province, but Yuan repeatedly enticed him with high-ranking positions, but he claimed illness and did not rise. When Song Jiaoren was assassinated, the righteous army in the south was about to rise again. The leaders of the people's party recommended Mr. Fan for the affairs of Wan, so he first sent Gong Zhenpeng to secretly attack Yingzhou and entered Wuhu himself, establishing a military government and sending troops to occupy Datong and pacify the prefectures along the Huai River to the north. When Nanjing collapsed, the righteous army was repeatedly defeated. He still coordinated with Bo Wenwei to advance and garrison Anqing, facing Yuan's army upstream. Then Wenwei's general, Hu Wantai, betrayed and responded to Ni Sichong, turning his guns to attack the military government. The whole city was terrified. Mr. Fan went straight out to die. A talented officer helped him board a boat to escape. After the righteous army had secretly joined Yuan's forces, the state and counties listed him as a wanted man and changed his name, fleeing to Japan. Not long after, he returned to Shanghai on the orders of President Sun to plan another uprising. At that time, Zheng Rucheng had occupied the Shanghai Arsenal and built several layers of trenches, fortifications, and cannons, repairing defenses, training soldiers, and inspecting weapons. The righteous army attacked with all its strength, but could not capture it. Mr. Fan and Chen Qimei plotted to overcome the difficulties to achieve their goal. Chen Yuanfu, a former servant of the arsenal, was a fellow townsman of Mr. Fan and respected him. He gathered more than ten comrades to join him and gradually gained influence, obtaining several hundred people. Mr. Fan encouraged them to remove its generals and officers and rise up to respond to Mr. Fan, but Mr. Fan held back and did not act. Rucheng's army was repeatedly alarmed at night. A spy informed Chen Yuanfu of the plot, and Yuanfu was killed. Mr. Fan's plan became more urgent. Rucheng was afraid and telegraphed Yuan. Yuan sent assassins to assassinate Mr. Fan at night. This was on the twentieth day of the ninth month of the third year of the Republic of China. Mr. Fan was generous, upright, courageous, and unusually righteous. He was also able to generously give money to the officers. At the Minli Bao newspaper, all his income was used to support his comrades, without using a single penny to support his family. He loved to collect books, and his collection was mostly of fine and rare editions. His finances were often insufficient, so he would sell thousands of the books he had collected, which was still not enough, and he would even pawn his curtains and mosquito nets. Therefore, the officers who came to join him all mourned his death. On the day of his death, there were those who wept uncontrollably.
