The first room features works by Western painting professors, including Principal Liu's recent masterpieces of Huangshan Mountain and West Lake, as well as Western landscape paintings of West Lake by professors Zhang Xian, Kang, Wang Yuanbo, Ni Yitao, and Chen Renhao. The second and third rooms feature Western landscape paintings, and the fourth room features watercolor paintings. All of the above are located in the Guanhai Pavilion. The fifth room features works by Chinese painting professors, including collaborative masterpieces by Principal Liu and professors Wang Gechou and Xie Gongzhan, as well as landscape and flower paintings by professors Li Jian, Zhu Leshan, Wu Fuyun, Xu Zhengbai, Ma Gongyu, Wang Shengyuan, and Zhang Tianqi. The sixth, seventh, and eighth rooms feature students' Chinese paintings. The ninth room features students' crafts, mostly practical items. The tenth room features inscriptions, calligraphy, paintings, and rubbings from various collectors and large bookstores for teachers and students to consult. All of the above are located in the Yihai Hall. Furthermore, the art museum in the Cuntian Pavilion displays mostly copies of European masters' famous works by Principal Liu from his time in Europe, as well as works by past and present professors of the school, all with detailed descriptions. Although the museum is usually open, it does not easily receive guests. This is a great opportunity for the public to visit. The high quality, richness, and well-organized arrangement of the exhibition surpass past exhibitions. The exhibition is open for two more days, today and tomorrow. People in Shanghai should not miss this opportunity.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Boy (1)(0)(3)

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"I know how to do it! Mr. Ha often uses this method! But because I didn't have camphor oil before, I only used a pin," Donn said, then gently dripped a drop on the insect's head. The pair of lake-colored wings vibrated for a moment and then became still. Before this little slaughter was finished, Tandy suddenly shouted from the bedroom, "Oh, the little crabs have come out, the big one has eaten them all." (Note) Xiao Qiao and his aunt went to the rescue, only to see Tandy jumping excitedly on a chair, while two small crabs were crawling around on the floor, having desperately escaped from the wire mesh of the cage. Another one was climbing towards the top of the cage, its life clearly under great threat, because a tragic and fascinating scene was unfolding below. The big crab retreated into a small house in the cage, which was where the Borley water glass used to be, and sat there calmly, eating one of its own kind, completely unmoved. The poor sufferer's claws were all pulled off, its body overturned, its upper shell held in a pincer, close to the big crab's mouth, serving as a plate. Then it used another pincer to scoop out the flesh of the sufferer and ate it leisurely, sometimes turning its strange and protruding eyes from one side to the other, extending a thin tongue to lick those eyes, causing the children to burst into laughter. Madam Shu sent the cage into Donn's room for him to observe this spectacle, while Xiao Qiao collected the escaped soldiers and locked them in an overturned washbasin.

(Note) "鮮" (xiān) is a homophone of the character "蟹" (xiè), meaning crab.

Shanghai Tennis Stars Qiu Feihai and Wang Wenzheng Win Performances in Hong Kong; Wang Wenzheng Defeats Lin Zhen Two Sets to Zero; Qiu and Wang Win Three Straight Against the Lin Zhen Brothers

Our country's tennis stars Qiu Feihai and Wang Wenzheng, etc., recently departed from Shanghai to compete in Southeast Asia. On the morning of the 16th, they arrived in Hong Kong on the President Jefferson liner. Coincidentally, Helen Wills Moody, the 1930 American junior women's singles and doubles champion, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing and traveled south on the same ship to visit the Philippines. Taking advantage of the stopover in Hong Kong, Qiu and the others competed at the Chinese Recreation Club for two days, resulting in complete victories. The results are as follows:

Qian Yaobin defeated Xu Runpei 6-4

Wang Wenzheng defeated Lin Zhen

American female tennis player Helen Wills Moody and He Jialiu played a doubles exhibition against Xu and Qian on the first day (16th). Speaking of the lady’s performance, the forehand shots were excellent, often passing over the net smoothly, with accurate placement and powerful serves, which are her strengths. The footwork was exceptionally agile, with a masculine style in posture and attitude. The backhand was also very good, with occasional strokes of great skill. The overhead smash was also commendable. In the second game, several unforced errors due to her speed gave Qian and Xu the opportunity to tie the score. It is said that the old Wang of the Chinese Recreation Club, once a top-notch singles player, may not be able to beat the lady. In the first singles match, Qian Yaobin played against Xu Runpei. Due to waiting for Wang Wenzheng, an extra game was added. Qian Yaobin's performance was mediocre, and neither side exerted much effort, so there was nothing exciting. The third match was between Wang Wenzheng and AS Lin Zhen, one being the runner-up in the Shanghai hard court tennis singles, and the other being the Hong Kong singles champion. The two heroes fought fiercely, with each set reaching 5-7 or higher. Their skills each had their own strengths. Wang Wenzheng has the nickname "Iron Horse" in Shanghai, known for his running and stamina. His baseline forehand and backhand strokes are his signature moves, and his footwork is very neat and calm, which are his strengths. He always aims and hits hard at the opponent's every shot, never slacking off from beginning to end. The key to his victory lies in this. His weak point is inaccurate slices, and his drop shots are not yet perfect. Therefore, he only hit one good drop shot in two sets. His victory over Lin Zhen was entirely due to the balls he placed left and right with his forehand and backhand, leaving the lively Lin Zhen exhausted. His losses were due to failed slices and drop shots. If Lin Zhen could use his strengths to attack Wang's weaknesses, serving more lobs and inducing Wang to slice and rushing to the net to make drop shots, he could have won the second set. It was already conceivable when he lost four straight games.

Qiu and Wang Also Win in Doubles

The 17th was the second day of the exhibition match, and the number of spectators was no less than the previous day. In the first match, Xu Runpei and Qian Yaobin played a singles match. Qian's performance was better than on the first day, with powerful forehand shots, but otherwise mediocre. It was indeed fortunate that he won fourth place in this year's All-China Games. Xu Hupei performed exceptionally diligently, showing considerable skill in serving and volleying, and defeated Qian Yaobin 2-0. The second match, the doubles between Qiu Feihai and Wang Wenzheng against the Lin Zhen brothers, was the most exciting. Wang's skills are indeed as good as described the previous day. Qiu Feihai's skills are even better than Wang's. His excellent forehand shots are his specialty, and his volleying and low shots are also his forte. He has rich experience and very sharp eyesight, able to discern the height, distance, and whether the opponent's shot is out of bounds at a glance, never missing one. It's a pity that his backhand is weak, with a very sharp angle, often resulting in out-of-bounds shots. His slices are also not yet perfect. There was a reason for his loss to Xu Chengji in this year's All-China Games. In doubles, Wang Wenzheng and he are well-coordinated, and against the Hong Kong doubles champions, the Lin Zhen brothers, they were indeed evenly matched. Therefore, the first set went to as high as 10-8. Both sides showed their full potential. The Lin Zhen brothers are well-coordinated, excelling in running, volleying, and high overheads. Qiu and Wang excel in low shots, baseline shots, accurate shots, and powerful shots. Therefore, they suppressed the ball and lobbed it high, and when the Lin Zhen brothers made high overheads, they hit it horizontally between the two of them, thus winning. Their ability to do so requires a deep understanding of the art of the game. As for the re-performance on Wednesday and Thursday, it can only be decided this afternoon. Whether the trip to Guangzhou will materialize will also be determined in the next day or two, pending a reply from the provincial government.

Industrial and Commercial Lending Still Faces Difficulties

In recent days, the business of the financial sector has developed slightly. Sound silver and money businesses and commercial firms have been communicating with each other regarding lending and credit transactions, etc., unlike the previous sluggishness. Even large amounts of money are being made complete by any means, and they are also gradually being replenished. Therefore, the recent situation has the appearance of recovery. However, most commercial settlements have not been completely saturated, and small problems have followed one after another. Since our country changed to legal tender, foreign trade has not been willing to use legal tender as the standard. The raw materials for imported goods that are in excess of exports are all rising sharply, regardless of whether they are fast-selling or slow-selling. However, several raw materials for domestic goods must be obtained from foreign countries. Therefore, with the price of raw materials rising, it is difficult to sell finished products cheaply. If you want to increase the value, it is difficult. Therefore, most factories that use foreign raw materials are half-handed and cannot develop. The silver and money industry is subject to various obstacles from foreign firms, so lending is naturally difficult. Special obstacles have also arisen in economic circulation. In addition, the end of the year is not far away, and timid people are mainly shrinking and unwilling to lend as much as possible. As a result, there are many more obstacles in the active money market. The foreign discount rate in the market is based on the old rules, opening at 1 jiao and 3 fen in both the morning and afternoon markets. The dividend is still white and there is no added water. Check transactions are still moderately simple and complex. The morning market transferred more than 3.4 million, and new transactions were more than 600,000. Afternoon market transactions were more than 100,000, and transactions in small general meetings were more than 800,000. More than 900,000 banknotes were issued in this port, and more than 1.4 million were shipped out. Foreign mortgage transactions were redeemed for more than 500,000, and more than 800,000 were newly made. The private banks' foreign public orders collected and delivered more than 52.2 million, and the foreign dividend orders collected and delivered more than 4.3 million, and various remittance orders more than 400,000. Yarn Flowers: Many Profiteers Cash Out, Yarn Flowers Suddenly Decline in the Afternoon, Extreme Rises and Falls are Quite Startling

The yarn market experienced rapid ups and downs, and the situation once again became volatile. Initially, banks and public bond groups increased their positions, causing market panic and unusual tension. This was because general speculators were overly enthusiastic, bullish on cotton yarn, due to depleted inventories and high raw cotton prices. Therefore, they aggressively bought forward contracts, with the last three months breaking the new record seen after November and April. The peak reached 208.9 yuan. In the afternoon, profiteers cashed out, and the price suddenly plummeted.

Forward Month Yarn Once Saw New High Prices

In the morning trading of standard yarn, the near month was slightly flat, with a small decrease of 0.3 to 0.4 yuan. The far month was auctioned at a high price, but the market situation was still firm. After two or three rounds of bidding, the price of raw cotton moved forward, and the trading floor suddenly became tense, with particularly strong buying interest. The bullish trend in the last three months became increasingly intense, with a major player continuing to buy. News of continued gains in public bonds further boosted sentiment, and new highs for the far month emerged one after another. The April contract approached the 210 yuan mark. At the close, Changfeng, Jinchang, and Dafu unanimously offered to sell, and the market situation slightly weakened. As a result, each month rose by 1.5, 1.6 to 2.1 yuan compared to the closing price on the 7th, except for the current month, which only rose by 0.4 yuan. The market suddenly declined in the afternoon, and the situation changed drastically. Large-scale selling by those who had profited in the morning led to sluggish sentiment, and selling pressure intensified. The market gradually declined step by step. After a surge of ten yuan in three days, there should have been this reaction. As a result, each month fell by 2 to 3.3 yuan compared to the morning closing price. Special Autumn Issue Chrysanthemum

Lament for "Chrysanthemums"

— (Meng Zhao)

Chrysanthemums are hermits, standing proudly in the frost, not competing with ordinary flowers for beauty. With integrity and a pure breeze, people compete to praise them.

However, I occasionally passed through bustling streets and saw signs saying "Chrysanthemums Cheap Sale."

I walked around to admire them and saw many good flowers, some slender and some plump, swaying gracefully. The prices were marked at 4, 6 cents, 1 yuan, and 2 yuan. I couldn't help but feel that famous chrysanthemums were being buried and felt sad for them.

Once a chrysanthemum is praised by a celebrity, its value increases tenfold, and it is供養 in a study. But once it falls into the hands of ordinary people, they use it as a tool to make money. It is just like a maiden from a respectable family who falls into a brothel, is abused by an evil madam, and is forced to stand on the street soliciting customers. Are there any Tao Yuanming enthusiasts who will rise up and become flower protectors?

Loving Chrysanthemums

— Xia Fei

Growing flowers was originally an elegant affair for cultured people. Although I don't have the qualifications of a cultured person, I still like these trinkets. So people often say that these are also elegant affairs, but in reality, I am not worthy of being called a cultured person, so how can there be any elegant affairs? Besides, I am not trying to learn to be a cultured person. This is just what my nature likes and what my heart loves.

In my courtyard, there are two flower beds. In addition to finding all kinds of exotic flowers and plants to transplant in them, I also look for various plants that are not easily seen to plant inside.

The flowers on the cart can be said to be continuous throughout the four seasons. No matter what season it is, there are several kinds of flowers and plants to enjoy. The four kinds of flowers that I usually like are: plum blossoms, orchids, lotus flowers, and chrysanthemums, and chrysanthemums are my favorite. Now, in my courtyard, there are more than a dozen kinds of chrysanthemums planted, a total of more than 30 pots, including red, yellow, purple, blue, white, lotus, light and dark, and combined colors. Although they cannot be called anything famous, they are still lovely. Because in addition to the "Blood Droplets", "Golden Plate承露", "Cranes Dancing in the Sky", "Night Fragrance", "Lion Ball", "Phoenix Tail", and "Peacock Screen" that are available in the market, there are also several kinds that I have named myself using the names of ancient poems. Such as: Mantingfang, Willow Yellow, Osmanthus Fragrance, Green Shirt Wet, Drunken Flower Yin, 相见欢, East Wind First Branch, Happy Moving Orioles, Exploring Spring, Butterfly Love Flower, West River Moon, etc., are all determined according to their color, nature and form.

In the past two years, however, I have had no time to cultivate them personally due to my career, so I have to entrust all the responsibilities to my wife, because my wife is a loyal comrade of my love of flowers.

Eating Chrysanthemums

— Zhou Xian

Chrysanthemums are noble scholars, so those who plant and appreciate chrysanthemums all become elegant people, and those who can compose poems about chrysanthemums are naturally even more noble.

When it comes to chrysanthemums, it seems that they are only for the appreciation and chanting of noble and elegant scholars. Little do they know that the petals of chrysanthemums are a very good food. My hometown is a rural village outside Suzhou. Although my hometown has never produced famous scholars or poets, every one of the more than 30 families in the village planted half a plot of autumn chrysanthemums. Planting chrysanthemums in my hometown was not for appreciation, but for the sole purpose of eating.

The most common way to eat them is to make chrysanthemum cakes. First, pick the petals of the blooming chrysanthemums, wash them, let them cool until they are half-dry, and then sugar-preserve them with osmanthus flowers, seal them in a bottle, and bury them underground. When they are opened in March and April of the following year, the petals have been completely preserved, and at the same time, the juice has a very rich mixed fragrance of chrysanthemums and osmanthus flowers. Use this sugar juice to mix into the flour, and use a printed version engraved with chrysanthemums to print the cakes piece by piece. There is no need to add any储子. After steaming, it is a fragrant chrysanthemum cake. Although the reason why chrysanthemum cake is famous is because it is usually printed with a chrysanthemum version, or because it is made with chrysanthemum brine, it is impossible to verify. Anyway, it is called chrysanthemum cake, which is very meaningful. If you want pure chrysanthemum juice, you only need to not mix it with osmanthus flowers when sugar-preserving it, but its taste is not as rich as that of osmanthus flowers, but the fragrance is more than that.

Crab powder chrysanthemum pot is also one of the chrysanthemum food methods in my hometown, but this is only used for banquets. First, stir-fry the crab powder, then pour in the prepared plump chrysanthemum petals. While pouring, lift the pot away from the fire, and stir it two or three times with quick hands. The deliciousness of crab, the fragrance of chrysanthemums, when eaten when the wine is half-drunk, there is really a benefit of refreshing and sobering up. The amount of chrysanthemum petals is most appropriate with two parts crab powder to one part chrysanthemum petals. If there is too much crab powder, the chrysanthemum辦 will be overcooked, and the fragrance will be reduced. If there are too many chrysanthemum 辦, it will make the eater's tongue feel bitter. In Shanghai, I have also eaten so-called chrysanthemum pot in a certain wine, but it is just sparse chrysanthemum petals floating on the dish. It is only a name, and each person only has ten or so strands on their mouths, and they can't taste any tea at all.

To offer chrysanthemums for people to gorge on, this may give elegant people a feeling of boiling cranes and burning琴, which seems to be a big disappointment. In fact, it is better to pick them when they are blooming and repair the five internal organs than to let the flowers bloom and wither and be trampled by people. Therefore, I especially introduce it to readers for a quick taste.

Good Colors of the East Hedge

— Juan Yin

Complaining for Chrysanthemums

— Qing Qu

There are the most types of chrysanthemums. The ancients called him "節花", which still makes some sense; because he bloomed when all the flowers were withering, and served as the last in the team of flowers. Isn't this kind of qualification worthy of admiration? It is also because he has endured severe frost and cold, and still stands independently, fighting against the north wind, without showing any weakness! So chrysanthemums bloom in many colors, and they are all very beautiful! Look, are there any wandering bees and butterflies to invade him at this time? Everyone knows that there will be none. Then, the rank of chrysanthemums is really several times higher than that of other ordinary flowers!

However, generally people who love chrysanthemums prefer to use chrysanthemums to symbolize women. I don't know why? Like "Powder Xishi", "Beautiful Face Change", "Drunk Concubine Yang", "Changing New Makeup", if you want to list this kind of nouns, there are really a lot. Now, if you find a rare famous chrysanthemum, no matter what kind of flower he is, hey! He will actually match the word "modern" and call it "Modern Chrysanthemum"; isn't this insulting the integrity of the chrysanthemum and the reputation inherited from the three paths of shrubs? Not enough, treat chrysanthemums like prostitutes, when they are in full bloom, display them in the middle of gold and paper, and force them to be smoked by wine and lights day and night. In a few days, alas! The color of the flowers has changed, and the branches and leaves have gradually withered and yellowed. Seeing the haggard appearance, people will naturally be disgusted. In the end, they will be abandoned to the side of the wall, and no one will pay attention to them anymore! You think, the life of chrysanthemums is so pitiful, I really feel injustice for him, and I want to use a pen to appeal.

What reason is there? Chrysanthemums are most suitable in the wilderness and between fences, so he has a chic and refined charm; if there is a clear stream reflecting it, and the rice paddies are like clouds, and the half-closed thatched door is on the outside, he would rather be close to the old farmers. This is the chrysanthemum's wish; even if there are no confidants to appreciate it, he can also freely eat the clouds and drink dew, and he can also leave a fragrance in his later years. Even if he braves the frost and rain, he is enough to be proud of himself in the world! If not, after suffering so much suffering, using bamboo branches to tie him and hemp threads to tie him up, like a prisoner, living in a dungeon every day, Chrysanthemum is holding a belly full of injustice, and wants to hope that people will rescue him.

Japanese Chrysanthemum Exhibition (Part 1)

— Ji Yun

Japanese chrysanthemums were originally introduced from our country. Although the variety is not as diverse as what we currently have, their cultivation methods are far superior. The reason is that the Japanese always maintain a dissatisfied attitude towards everything, constantly striving for improvement. There are many chrysanthemum research groups, the most famous being the Akikoka, Jugukai, and Choseikai, etc. They have branches in various places, and their activities are very developed. Each exhibition centers around Hibiya Park.

Everyone in our country knows that cherry blossoms are the national flower of Japan, but this is actually wrong. Cherry blossoms are merely a unique flower and tree to Japan, and they are popular among the Japanese people due to their beautiful color. The national flower of Japan is the chrysanthemum. Their medals often have yellow chrysanthemum patterns, which are symbols of the national flower.

Japan categorizes chrysanthemums into three sizes: large, medium, and small. Our country's pink lotus and unicorn horn, etc., with larger flower heads, belong to the large chrysanthemum category. Cloud Phoenix, Crane Dance Cloud Zero, etc., with smaller flower heads, are classified as medium chrysanthemums, while others such as longan and aster are small chrysanthemums. The naming of chrysanthemums in Japan is also the same as in our country, each based on their own meaning, without any fixed rules. Generally, flowers with broad petals are called "lotus," while spherical flowers with clustered petals are called "thick objects." Flowers with tubular and swirling petals are called "embracing." Petals are divided into three types: tubular petals, spoon petals, and flat petals. The evaluation criteria are divided into eleven categories: color, luster, flower body, flower shape, petal quality, character, talent, strength, flower stem, leaves, and future. Those selected into grades are awarded gold cups, silver cups, certificates, etc. by the association, all of which are considered to be the highest honor.

The posture of large and medium chrysanthemums cultivated in Japan can be divided into two types: one is ordinary potted plants, and the other is the landscape arrangement of our country. There is no fixed form for landscape arrangements, which is the same as in our country. One chrysanthemum plant has hundreds of flowers, arranged into various forms, seeking beauty and neatness. Potted plants are entirely for appreciation and evaluation, so they are the most exquisite. Each pot of chrysanthemum has at least three branches, forming a triangle with the same height. Our country's precious chrysanthemums often only have one independent branch, which is not the case there. From a young age, the branches are divided into three parts, and they try their best to cultivate them to grow. The mud pot is about one foot high and seven or eight inches in diameter. If the pot is small, the flower will be thin, which is why chrysanthemum growers in our country must liberate the flower pots. The flower stem is thick and tall, more than three feet, supported by purple bamboo, so the branches are straight, with no side branches. The leaves are fat and dense, from the roots to the top of the stem, there is not a single leaf that has fallen off or turned yellow. In our country, we mostly only use manure for fertilization, which seems insufficient, and scientific methods must be used. When fertilizing, the gardeners often accidentally stain the roots and leaves with fertilizer, causing the roots and leaves to often scorch and fall off. Also, the flower pots are low and small, placed on the ground, and rainwater splatters mud onto the leaves, blocking the fine pores that absorb nutrients, which also easily leads to scorching and falling off. Therefore, the flower pots must be tall and large, and it is not necessary to place them on the ground to receive ground energy. Chrysanthemums like sunlight but fear sunburn, so it is advisable to put them in a flower shed.

After seeing the Japanese chrysanthemums, I feel that our country's chrysanthemums are delicate and somewhat sickly. Their chrysanthemums have three branches that are equally developed, and the flowering time is the same, without any distinction. The corolla is large and fat, reaching six or seven inches in diameter, and the spherical ones are hemispherical, unlike our country's which are flat and small. The petals are thick and fat, and the luster is also good. A cardboard or circular lead wire frame is placed under the flower to prevent the petals from falling down and damaging the flower's posture. If there are more than three branches, the arrangement also has a certain format, with approximately a pentagon or hexagon being the most common.

A New Chapter in Appreciating Chrysanthemums at Guyi Garden

— Meng Fei

The magnificent garden is called Guyi,

With famous historical sites in Chaxi (i.e., Nanxiang).

Since the new renovation last year,

It has been cleaned up, splendid and picturesque.

There are many exotic varieties of famous flowers in all seasons,

And century-old trees are rare in the world.

The artificial mountains are stacked into immortal caves,

Ingenious and exquisite, with upper and lower ladders.

The Five Old Peaks resemble the postures of five old men,

With different lengths, and distinctions between thin and fat.

The Nine-Bend Bridge has only three curves,

Where you can sit and watch the fish leap and the kites fly.

There is the Phoenix Terrace, and the Fishing Rock,

And bamboo branches and green bamboos ripple.

Next to the Plum Blossom Hall, plum blossoms are planted,

And white cranes perch in the White Crane Pavilion.

An unmoored boat is docked by the pond,

And the decorations in the boat are even more exquisite.

Therefore, tourists gather like clouds all year round,

Holding hands in front of the flowers, laughing and talking softly.

Today, the sky is clear and the clouds are leisurely, with good autumn colors,

And yellow flowers fill the eyes with a riot of colors,

Snow Lion, Drunken Concubine Yang,

Kirin Belt, Phoenix Robe,

All are extraordinary and new flowers, showing their strangeness.

They are stacked into several flower mountains,

Dazzling the eyes and captivating the mind,

The public exhibition is free of charge,

And the scheduled time is half a month.

Presumably, a generation of Yuanming with a chrysanthemum obsession,

Will surely enter the garden together,

To appreciate the famous flowers and comment on them.

Casual Talks on Chrysanthemum Cultivation

— (Ying Dai)

As autumn is about to end, chrysanthemums are blooming again. Among all flowers, the chrysanthemum's character has always been respected by poets and elegant scholars. Therefore, when chrysanthemums are in full bloom, people from all over hold chrysanthemum appreciation gatherings. Just in Shanghai, various gardens and amusement parks are busy opening chrysanthemum exhibitions. However, chrysanthemums are not easy to cultivate. If the same chrysanthemum plant is grown by two different people, the plant's form and the flower size will be completely different. Whether it is good or bad depends on the cultivation method. As chrysanthemums are blooming, to add some color to autumn, I will briefly describe some chrysanthemum cultivation methods that I know of:

Cutting: Cutting is the most common method. If the roots of last year's withered chrysanthemums are not removed, after Qingming Festival, buds will sprout from the roots, becoming new chrysanthemums. In April or May, after the chrysanthemum buds have grown, we will pluck the tops and insert them into the soil. In a few days, they will take root and come alive. Most chrysanthemum growers adopt this method.

Old Rootstock: The old rootstock of the chrysanthemum will also sprout after it withers and turns yellow. If we do not pluck them and let them grow, adding more fertilizer, they can grow three or four feet tall, and the flowers can be as big as a hat. However, chrysanthemum enthusiasts only occasionally use old rootstocks to cultivate large flowers and will not grow all chrysanthemums in this way.

Seedling: Many people know that chrysanthemums do not have seeds, but they actually do. After the large flowers wither, the collected flower seeds will sprout when sown in the soil the following year, and the flowers that bloom may be completely different from the original color and petals. It can bloom badly, but it can also bloom exceptionally well. The so-called new varieties are mostly from seedlings. Chrysanthemum enthusiasts often try to obtain new varieties.

Fertilization: To have large flowers when chrysanthemums bloom, sufficient fertilizer is indispensable. For chrysanthemums, bean cake and grass juice are generally the best fertilizers. Initially, they should be planted in the ground to obtain earth energy. Only when they are about to bloom can they be dug up with the soil and moved into flower pots. If they are planted in pots early on, they will not be very robust.

Catching Insects: During the growth period of chrysanthemums, in addition to early weather that may cause death, green caterpillars are also a major enemy. Therefore, in summer and autumn, we must inspect the chrysanthemum garden one by one every morning and evening. If we find any insect damage, we must immediately catch the small insects. Otherwise, if the branches and leaves are damaged, they will not grow easily, and may even die.

Pinching: When chrysanthemums are not growing, in May and June, we should also pinch off the tops. This will allow small heads to grow, and each head will have a flower. You leave as many heads as you want flowers. The small branches attached to the side should also be pinched off. However, it is best to have four or five flowers on a chrysanthemum plant. Too few is not good-looking, and too many will not grow big. It is not suitable. In August and September, when the flower buds are just sprouting, if we find that the side branches and leaves also have flower buds, we should remove them immediately to avoid too many flowers and difficulty in growing them big.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talking

Silk Material Shortage Forces Shutdowns

— Xin Xin

A report states: "Several silk factories in this city that had commenced operations have recently had to suspend production due to a lack of raw materials, rendering them unable to reel silk. As of last month, sixteen factories have already ceased operations, and by the end of this month, it is feared that all will be forced to shut down."

According to a prominent figure in the silk industry, the reason for the "lack of raw materials" is that "in recent years, due to the global economic recession and the dumping of cheap Japanese silk, Chinese silk has suffered a setback, with prices plummeting. As a result, silkworm farmers in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang regions, finding it unprofitable, have turned to other occupations. However, since the beginning of this summer, the silkworm-producing areas in Japan have suffered from floods, reducing output, while demand from Europe and America has increased, leading to active sales and rising silk prices." Nevertheless, while on the one hand "sales are active and silk prices are rising," on the other hand, because "silkworm farmers are raising very few silkworms, resulting in low production," the "great turnaround in Chinese silk exports" has ultimately been thwarted by a "lack of raw materials," forcing shutdowns. Consequently, the silk industry is requesting the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction to pay attention to two points: "First, increase the distribution of silkworm eggs. This year, only over 1.8 million sheets of improved silkworm eggs were distributed. Next year, at least 6 million sheets must be distributed to ensure that production and sales are balanced. Second, cultivate mulberry forests. In recent years, silkworm farmers, because they have witnessed the sharp decline in silk prices, view silkworm farming with dread, and not only do they not cultivate the mulberry trees they have planted, but they are also cutting them down on a large scale, resulting in insufficient silkworm feed and causing panic." At the same time, the silk industry itself has decided to "improve technology."

The reason for the decline of the national silk industry in recent years, as a certain silk industry magnate said, is "due to the global economic recession and the dumping of cheap Japanese silk." However, why can others "dump prices," while we alone cannot "lower" prices? Speaking of which, our history of silkworm farming is longer than theirs.

The reason, in short, is that our silkworm farmers adhere to old methods in everything they do, without knowing how to research or apply scientific methods. As a result, even silkworm eggs have to be bought from them as "improved varieties," and other things are even more imaginable. Not only is the method of silkworm farming like this, but even worse is that they are helped by the government and adopt collective methods, while we still rely on individual silkworm farmers with their meager strength to "fight on their own."

Due to different economic structures and methods, may I ask, how can they not be "forced" to "turn to other occupations," how can they succeed?

Furthermore, regarding this year's "active sales and rising silk prices," this is also the result of occasional good timing and location. Therefore, the silk industry's hope for the two points from the Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provincial Department of Construction also feels too distant. Whether increasing the number of silkworm eggs from over 1.8 million sheets to 6 million sheets will cause problems in the supply of mulberry leaves will be discussed later, but whether the result of 6 million sheets of silkworm eggs will lead to accumulation and difficulty in selling should be considered first. Not long ago, didn't we see news about people fearing that cocoons would hatch into moths and being unable to afford warehouse rent? As for the second point, that depends on the "increase or decrease in market prices." If there is confidence in production, then there is no need for the Department of Construction to pay attention; the silkworm farmers themselves will quickly restore it to its former appearance. Otherwise, no matter how much attention the Department of Construction pays, since they have "turned to other occupations," they will naturally "cut down the useless mulberry trees on a large scale."

Currently, the most crucial question is how to compete with others in the world market. Other minor issues must all be determined by how the crucial question can be resolved.

Madman

— Lin Na

The sunlight had already crept over the window seam, stealingly hanging on the white ash wall, reflecting a few purple-red lines, intricately, silently.

Widow Ma's cuckoo clock had already sounded seven times. Her daughter-in-law, Wang Wanglao, was already busily clanging and banging things in the kitchen, muttering, cursing as if in a dream, starting with cursing the weather, then the kitten for being disobedient and not letting her sleep well at night, and then her mother-in-law, her husband for being gluttonous and lazy, a long string of complaints, as if telling someone: then the sound of straw rustling, the sound of striking a lighter, followed by the crackling sound of flames.

As usual, at this time, most of the students would already be standing under the lychee tree with their schoolbags on their backs, shouting loudly:

"Mr. Lin, the sun is shining on your butt!"

But now it was past seven o'clock, and although the weather was cold, the good sun was still… and the lychee tree

Page 18

was still so quiet.

Suddenly, a burst of clamor came from the corner of the village, laughter, shouts, calls, curses overflowing in a团, and the noise was getting closer and closer, clearer and louder. I was suspicious and got up and looked out through the window seam. I saw people crowded on the hexagonal wall, a bald-headed, bare-chested young farmer running in front, mad and delirious, holding a bamboo flute high in his hand, shouting and cursing loudly, tears in his eyes, calling in a hoarse voice:

"Arbitration? Good! Go find Mr. Lin!"

Behind him followed a large group of people, village school students, old people, children, and several nosy women. They kept their distance, laughing, shouting, and yelling, "Madman!" But when he stopped and waved at them, everyone hurried backward, running around in a panic.

They crowded toward where I lived. Widow Ma's daughter-in-law ran up from the kitchen in a panic to tell me; "Mr. Lin, the madman, with his head tilted, is banging on the door, insisting on seeing you!"

The knocking on the door rang loudly, and the madman, with his head tilted, howled with a sobbing, shrill voice:

"Mr. Lin! Mr. Lin, I want to see Mr. Lin!"

Then came another burst of clamor and laughter from the crowd. So I put on my clothes and went out. The door opened, and the crowd erupted in enthusiastic cheering. The madman, with his head tilted, stood in front of me, full of grievances, tears shimmering in his eyes, pointing at the people who lived with him and wailing:

"Mr. Lin, please judge, they are bullying me, saying they want to steal my bamboo flute."

I knew his madness had flared up again today. One cannot oppose madmen. Therefore, I pretended to be angry, widened my eyes, and shouted at the village students:

"Why are you bullying him? What time is it? Why aren't you properly going to school for me!" So the students quietly dispersed in fear. Those who had squeezed in to watch the fun, based on past experience, knew that after the madman found the teacher for arbitration, there would be nothing special or new to watch, so they also trickled away in twos and threes. In the end, only he and I remained.

We sat on the roots of the lychee tree to bask in the sun. With his head still hanging so dejectedly, it seemed that his soul was no longer attached to his body.

Just a few months ago, who wouldn't have given him a thumbs-up and praised him as a "typical" farmer! Pure and honest, but now he was a madman. When he was fifteen years old, his father died, and his older brother sent him to work in a relative's house in another village, peacefully passing his days in work. It had been seven or eight years now. In these seven or eight years of unpaid labor, he had obtained the relative's permission to marry a cousin. But a few months ago, he was sent to another county to buy sugarcane seedlings, and when he returned home, he discovered that his cousin had been secretly married to a farmer in a neighboring village. Although he was heartbroken, he didn't say anything, just secretly shed tears, and didn't want to do anything, ate very little, and didn't sleep well at night, just like a ghost clutching a bamboo flute, talking to himself, groping in the dark to his cousin's husband's house; so he sat on the opposite ridge of the field and played the bamboo flute with melancholy, sighing and wailing, all night long...

But one night, he was beaten severely because his cousin's husband discovered that their newly acquired wife was disturbed by the flute sounds all night and felt uneasy. From then on, he went mad and returned to the village he had left seven or eight years ago. Now he was Madman Yaitou.

We were both immersed in the intoxication of memories. After a while, he sighed deeply and unknowingly began to cry sadly.

"Why are you crying?" I asked suspiciously.

"Crying?" He widened his eyes and looked at me in surprise, then sobbed, "People are all bullying me!" He stood up and strode toward the locust tree.

Soon, in the gentle air, the sound of the flute wafted from afar.

Water Flower

— Simon

A gentle night, cloaked in a deep ink-colored sky twinkling with stars. The river surface, filled with exquisite boats, is also filled with the lively sounds of songs and strings, gentle laughter, and low whispers of affection, dissolving into the bustling space, thinly spreading out, floating on the bright river surface.

The boat, like a forest, shot out brilliant lamp flowers, reflecting the water surface with countless window shadows, shimmering with gorgeous waves. The water undulates in the small wind, gently lapping against the boat strings, making rhythmic echoes; retreating, and kissing the river bank, colliding and spraying a string of white waves.

On the riverbank: the translucent contours of high-rise buildings proudly insert into the half-sky, trams clang, driving back and forth like long snakes.

The car brings various tourists. A small commotion rises at the riverside. A big worker stood on the deck and waved his hand:

"Sir, sit here. Are you waiting for the number one boat?"

"Sir, sit here. Are you waiting for the number one boat?"

Some jumped ashore to solicit business.

Then the boat loaded tourists and swam to the boat area in the heart of the river.

At this time, on the windows of each boat, the girls decorated like flowers stretched out their heads, with a seductive smile hanging on their faces. They waved with small red and green handkerchiefs.

The boat gradually approached.

"Sir, we have the best fragrant tea inside. Please come up and have some fun!"

"Sir, we have the best fragrant tea inside. Please come up and have some fun!"

So clear and melodious voices sounded together.

After a moment of chaos, it calmed down. Then came the sound of rowing and splashing water, and many boats sailed away separately, accompanied by even more moving singing, clear string music, and the joy of business.

The river surface revealed a large expanse of river water, lying under the moonlight.

The boat loaded people from the riverbank to the boats on the river, and then went back empty, and loaded people again in a moment. She was so busy like a shuttle. As the boats sent to and fro, the girls also had busy businesses, receiving new guests and sending off old ones. The girls' feelings were vaguely inlaid with some familiar and strange faces and eyes. Pressing their lips to each tourist's lips, their bodies fell into each tourist's chest. Late at night, the tourists emptied their pockets, took a boat to shore with a drunken daze, as if in a dream. Then the girls' wallets bulged up, their heads leaned out from the booth, and they said from a distance:

"Please come early tomorrow!" Then giggle.

The east gradually revealed fish belly white, and the scattered boats gathered back to the original place in succession. The singing and string music were sparse, and the noisy scene on the river suddenly became silent. Only a few night shift boats were lit.

Although there were so many boats on this river, there were even more people on yachts. The girls all had regular customers, who were permanent customers, and there were also occasional visitors who came on a whim. So the girls don't worry about no one coming, but are afraid of not being able to welcome them. Especially in the hot summer, the night breeze on the river is cool, and the air is fresh. Sitting on the boat, carrying a boat of moonlight and strings, listening to the girl's musical and intoxicating songs. Floating on the river, it's like a dream! Therefore, there are so many people on yachts, as long as after dusk, tourists will run in groups of three or five, and the boat picking up guests will be busy until midnight. If you come a little later, you won't be able to hire a boat with money.

Summer is a very pleasant and anticipated time for the girls.

At that time, in the prosperous time, the highest yacht fee was five yuan, and the cheapest one cost two silvers. Overnight expenses are historically harsh. You can also bring it ashore, and the cost will naturally be higher, but this situation is rare, because a yacht trip is for the scenery on the lake.

However, despite this, tourists have never decreased.

Days passed in a series, and the girls were the same on the water. There were still lively sounds of songs and strings on the water, but it was so quiet, and there was no gentle laughter, only empty boats carrying sorrow.

The prosperity on the water flowed away with the water.

The girls are still dressed like flowers, but there are fewer objects to appreciate. They still leaned on the window, staring, but with a sad look.

The boats picking up guests were also idle and flustered.

Why did the tourists suddenly fall to a terrible degree? Maybe they don't understand. After looking around for a long time, there was no sound on the quiet river. After a long time, I saw the boat swaying over with people, barely causing a commotion, but so few people, so many boats. What's the use? Moreover, now all those who come are regular customers with a purpose, who cannot be robbed.

Then a heavier sigh flew out of the river.

The girls lost their smiling faces, joy replaced sorrow, the songs and strings have gradually cooled down, and turned into a bitter complaint.

Gloomy shadows, bleak days, the girls dressed like flowers gradually withered. The boats floating on the water decreased day by day. Rain pattered outside the curtains, spring was waning, the silk quilt could not withstand the cold of the fifth watch, I didn't know I was a guest in a dream, I always enjoyed myself!

Jiang Zhe Bank Building Completion and Opening Commemorative Special Issue

Editor's Foreword

The Jiang Zhe Bank Building has gone through a construction period of two years and has only completed its final work today. That towering, magnificent new building at the corner of Jiangxi Road and Tianjin Road is the Jiang Zhe Bank Building that has been completed after two years of work.

Today is the first day that the bank has moved into its new building to conduct business. This is a day worth commemorating! We review the glorious history of the bank in the past, and it has completed a great mission in its gradual progress. Today, while we celebrate, we have even greater expectations for the future of the bank.

As a member of the Shanghai Banking Association, the bank upholds a stable business policy, uses its strong capital to support the advancement of industry and commerce. The bank's chairman Wu Qiding and directors Chen Jian'an, Du Yuesheng, Zhu Kongyang, Zhang Xiaolin, Zhu Yicai, Jin Tingsun, Sheng Pinchen, Liu Jisheng, Xu Boxiong, Zhou Wenrui, etc., are all financial giants. This kind of intelligence and financial strength tells us the fact that the bank has already embarked on a bright road. However, in today's extremely depressed industrial and commercial environment, they must rely on the support of the financial community, which is extremely important. We hope that the bank will, based on its past business policy, make ordinary adjustments to industry and commerce! In that case, not only will society benefit from it, but also the future of the nation will be deeply dependent on it.

Here, the editor expresses its infinite blessings to the bank and hopes that it will strive to complete its greater mission!

Shan Hai Marble Factory

Modern architecture. Beauty is important. Therefore, surface decoration projects. Then it is valued by people. Regarding the materials used in surface decoration projects. Such as cement. Artificial stone. And magnetic materials, etc. There are many types. However, the most valuable among them. And the most popular. Is marble. Because it is smooth and uniform. Strong and durable. With natural color patterns. Extremely rich and beautiful. Used for surface decoration. Both extremely magnificent and grand. And extremely economical and cost-effective. Because once installed. It lasts for a long time. It is not like ordinary surface decoration materials that are eroded by wind and rain. Easy to damage. Because it has this kind of advantage. The need for marble. Then, with the progress of the times. And become more urgent day by day. Shan Hai Marble Factory. Is the largest stone factory in our country. The factory site is located at the intersection of Xietu Road and Luban Road, Nanshi. Founded for many years. The manager is Mr. Su Guangming from Yunjian. Well managed. Thriving. The factory initially used domestic marble. Compete with imported products. Then, because the marble raw materials were not very large. And the color could not be harmonized. Not suitable for use in construction projects. The factory directly ordered large blocks of stone of various colors from Italy and other countries. The factory saws and polishes it by itself. And to extremely fine carvings. In order to achieve magnificent architecture. Now all the marble projects of the Jiang Zhe Building. Are all contracted by the factory. The factory has contracted in the past China Reclamation Bank. Fuyuan Bank, etc. Engineering stone materials. All have good results. According to the factory, it covers an area of more than five acres. Equipped with 30 machines. All kinds of equipment. Are all perfect. Specially hired experts to supervise. It can produce 20,000 square feet of polished sheets per month.

Interior View of Vault

The Door and Walls of a House

— Written by Heng You Pan, Translated by Chen Yin

Recently, houses and gardens have generally attracted attention to some extent, but there are still many people who are relatively indifferent to the discussion of doors and walls, which influence the appearance of houses and give the initial impression of houses.

The first thing that pedestrians or visitors on the street notice can be said to be the door and the wall. According to the design of these two, the taste and character of the owner and even the family can also be understood. Some houses are very spectacular and the interior decoration is very clever, but if they give an unpleasant first impression, there will be dissatisfaction with the house or garden.

However, it is not necessary to spend extravagant and disproportionate expenses just to decorate for this purpose. In suburban residences, garden cities, etc. in the United States and Britain, there are absolutely no specially made doors and walls, and some freely open a part of the garden. And to construct these, the first thing to pay attention to is the appearance, that is, low hedges that can be freely viewed from the outside of the garden or simply use fences, only to the extent of marking the boundary.

On the contrary, the doors and walls of Japan have always sacrificed appearance. High, closed walls are built so that they cannot be seen through from the outside and cannot be invaded, with the aim of monopolizing the peace of the residence. Even today, there are still glass shards or fifty nails buried on top of concrete walls. This is also a common occurrence. However, although these are used to prevent intruders, the beauty of the appearance is completely lost.

Today, architecture is gradually being improved, and Western-style architecture is becoming more and more popular, so this should be felt as an error of the earliest era.
